          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.1">athāto dvivraṇīyaṃ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.3">dvau vraṇau bhavataḥ | śarīrasamutthaś cāgantuś ca tayoḥ
            śarīrasamuttho vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātanimitta āgantukaḥ
            puruṣamṛgapaśupakṣivyāḍasarīsṛpapatanapīḍanaprahārā<cb/>gniviṣaasthisakalakapālakhaḍgacakreṣu
            paraśuśaktikuntādyāyudhaprahareṇābhighātanimittaḥ<lb/> | tatra tulye vraṇasāmānye
            dvikāraṇotthānaprayojanasāmarthyā<cb/>d dvivraṇīyaḥ ity ucyate |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.4">sarvvasminn eva cāgantau vraṇe tat kālam eva kṣatoṣmaṇaḥ |
            prasṛtasyaupaśamārtham pi<lb/>ttavacchītakriyāvibhāgaḥ | sandhānārthañ ca
            madhughṛtopayoga i<cb/>ti | etad vikāraṇotthānaprayojanam uttarakālan tu
              doṣopaplavaviśeṣā<hi>d avasthāntaraviśeṣāḥ</hi> śārīravat pratīkāraḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.5">doṣopaplavaviśeṣaḥ punaḥ samāsa<cb/>taḥ pañcadaśaprakāro bhavati |
            yathokte vraṇapraśnādhyāye prasaraṇasāmarthyāc cha<unclear>ddhaś ceti</unclear>
            ṣoḍaśaprakāra ity ucyate |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.6">tasya lakṣaṇaṃ dvividhaṃ | sāmānyalakṣaṇam viśeṣalakṣaṇañca | tatra
            vraṇe vṛṇotīti vraṇaḥ | viśeṣalakṣaṇampunarvvātādisvalakṣaṇaviśeṣaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.7">tatra śyāvāruṇābha<pb n="200r"/>bhastanu
            śītapicchilālpasrāvīrūkṣaścaṭacaṭāyanaśīlaḥ sphuraṇāyām atodabhedavedanāvahulo

            sthūloṣṭhaḥ stavdhasirāsnāyujālāvanaddhaḥ kaṭhinaḥ pāṇḍvāvabhāso mandavedanaḥ |
            śuklaśītasā<lb/>ndrapicchilāsrāvī guruś ceti kaphāt || pravālānalanicaya<cb/>prakāśaḥ

            ceti vātapittābhyāṃ || kaṇḍūyanaśīlaḥ sanistodavā<unclear>trū</unclear>kṣaḥ kharastaddho
            muhu<lb/>rmmuhuḥ śītapicchalāsrāvī ceti vātaśleṣmābhyāṃ || guruḥ sa<cb/>dāhoṣṇaḥ
            pītapāṇḍusrāvī ceti pittaśleṣmābhyāṃ || tanurūkṣastodavahulaḥ prasupta iva ca
              kṛṣṇāru<unclear>ṇā</unclear><lb/> bhastadvvarṇṇasrāvī ceti vātaśoṇitābhyāṃ ||
            ghṛtamaṇḍābho mīnadhāvanagandhīmṛdurvvisarppīkṛṣṇoṣṇasrāvī ceti pittaśoṇitābhyāṃ ||
            rakto gurusnigdhaḥ kaṇḍūprāyaḥ picchilaḥ sara<pb n="200v"/>ktasrāvī ceti
            śleṣmaśoṇitābhyāṃ | sphuraṇatodadāhadhūmāyanaprāyaḥ pītatanuraktasrāvī ceti
            vātapittaśoṇitebhyaḥ || kaṇḍūsphuraṇacumucumāyamānaprāyaḥ pāṇḍutanuraktasrā<lb/>vī ceti
            vātaśleṣmaśoṇitebhyaḥ || dāhapākarāgakaṇḍūprāyaḥ pā<cb/>ṇḍūraktapītāsrāvī ceti
            pittaśleṣmaśoṇitebhyaḥ || vividhadoṣavarṇṇavedanāsrāvaviśeṣopetaḥ pavanapittakaphebhyaḥ
            ||
            nirddarśakanirmmathanasphuraṇatodadāhapā<cb/>karāgakaṇḍū<unclear>vāṃ</unclear>svāpavahulo
            nānāvidhavarṇṇavedanāsrāvaviśeṣopetaḥ pavanapittakaphaśoṇi<lb/>tebhya iti ||
            jihvātalābho mṛdu ślakṣṇaḥ snigdho vigatavedanaḥ<cb/> suvyavasthito nirāsrāvaś ceti
            śuddho vraṇaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.8">tasyaitasya vraṇasya ṣaṣṭirupakramā bhavanti |
            tadyathā<lb/>patarpaṇamālepanaḥ pariṣeko 'bhyaṅgaḥ svedo vimlāyanam upanā<cb/>ho

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.1"> athātaḥ sadyovraṇacikitsitaṃ <lb n="6"/>vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.10">vaiśadyam anne 'bhiruciṃ saumanasyaṃ karoti ca ||
            <caesura/>
            <add place="inline">snigdhāṃ śuṣkāṃś ca daśanāṃ jihvāyāpi ca lāghavaṃ |</add>
            <caesura/>
             na cātigalatālvoṣṭhajihvārogasamudbhavaḥ |</l>

            sa mṛduḥ | madhūcchiṣṭamiva lepayati yatra<lb n="2"/>bheṣajaṃ sa cikkanaḥ | phenātimātra

            nasyāñjanīyaścikkaṇaḥ | vastisnehāḥ kharacikkaṇa iti ||</l>

            <caesura/>

            />kalkacūrṇṇasnehenānyatamasya mātrām pāyayitvā vāmayet |

              agni<lb n="2"/>taptair upaspṛśyamānaṃ muhūrttamupekṣeta | tatra pravṛttaṃ
            hṛllāsaṃ<cb/> jñātvā jānumātrāsanopaviṣṭam anyena hṛtpṛṣṭhayoḥ pāṇibhyām upari

            saṃśodhayed</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.39.33"> tathāṅgapragrahaṃ ghoram indriyāṇāñ ca vibhramaṃ ||
            <caesura/>
             ci<lb n="5"/>rāsanān tathā sthānāc chroṇyām bhavati vedanā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.39.34"> aticaṅkrama<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><cb/>ṇād vāyur jjaṃghorvvoḥ
            kurute rujāḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             sakthnoḥ praśoṣaṃ śopham vā pādaharṣam athāpi vā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.39.35a"> śīta<lb n="6"/>sambhogatoyānāṃ sevā mārutavṛddhaye ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.39.35b"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.39.36"> vātātapābhyāṃ vaivarṇṇyaṃ jvaram vāpi ni<subst>
              <del rend="no mark for deletion">ga</del>
              <add place="below">ya</add>
            </subst>cchati |
            <caesura/>
             niruddhādhyaśanāt mṛtyum vyādhim vā ghoram arcchati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.39.37"> asātmyabhojanād dhanyā<pb n="318v"/><lb n="1"/>d
              balavarṇṇā<unclear reason="looks like ca">va</unclear>saṃśayaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             anātmavantam paśuvad bhuñjate ye pramāṇataḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             rogānīkasya te mūlam ajīrṇṇāt prāpnuvanti ha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.39.38"> vyāpadāt kāraṇam vīkṣya vyāpatsv eteṣu buddhimān <lb n="2"/>|
            <caesura/>
             prayatetāturārogyai pratyanīkena hetunā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.39.39"> viriktavāntair hariṇaiṇalāvakāḥ śaśāś ca sevyāḥ samayūratittirāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saṣaṣṭikāś cāpi purāṇaśālayas ta<lb n="3"/>thaiva mudgā laghu yac ca kīrttitam iti
            ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer"> || cikitsāsthāne ekonacatvāriṃśattamo dhyāyaḥ ||</p>

             valīpa<lb n="5"/>litakhālityavyaṅgānāñ cāpy asambhavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.56"> tailaṅ kaphe ca vāte ca<metamark function="yati">,,</metamark>
            <cb/>kevalam pavane vasāṃ <metamark function="yati">,</metamark> |
            <caesura/>
             dadyān nastaḥ sadā pitte <metamark function="yati">,</metamark> sarppirmajjāsamārute
              <metamark function="yati">,,</metamark>|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.57"> caturvidhasya snehasya <metamark function="yati">,,</metamark>
            <lb n="6"/>vidhir eṣa prakīrttitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śleṣmasthānāvirodhitvāt teṣu tailam viśiṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.44"> avapīḍan tu śirovirecanavad
            abhiṣyaṇṇasarppadaṣṭamūrcchitavisaṃjñebhyo dadyāc chirovirecana<pb n="323r"/><lb n="1"
            />dravyāṇām anyatamam āsādyāvapīḍam iṣyateti | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.46"> cetovikārakrimiviṣābhipannānāñ cūrṇṇaṃ pradhamed iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.44a"> śarkarekṣurasakṣīrā <metamark function="yati">,</metamark>
            ghṛtamāṃsarasam pṛthak |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīṇānān nastato <lb n="2"/> dadyād raktapittagadeṣu ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.58"> || ataḥ param pravakṣyāmi <metamark function="yati">,</metamark>
            ka<cb/>vaḍagrahaṇe vidhiṃ <metamark function="yati">,</metamark> |
            <caesura/>
             caturddhā kavaḍasnehī prasādī śodhiropaṇau <metamark function="yati">,</metamark>|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.59"> sngidhoṣṇaiḥ snaihiko vāte <metamark function="yati">,</metamark>
            <g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/>
            <lb n="3"/>svāduśītaiḥ prasādanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pitte kaṭvamlalavaṇai <metamark function="yati">,</metamark> rūkṣaiḥ saṃśo<g
              ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><cb/>dhanaḥ kaphe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.60"> kaṣāyatiktamadhuraiḥ kaṭūṣṇo ropaṇo vraṇe <metamark
              function="yati">,</metamark>
            <caesura/>
             || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.61"> tatra trikaṭukāśitasarṣapasiddhārthakaka<lb n="4"/>lkam āloḍya
            tailamūtrakṣārasurāśukramadhūnām anyatamena salava<cb/>ṇam abhiprataptam
            upasvinnamṛditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśe dhārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.62"> sukhaṃ sañcāryate yā tu <lb n="5"/>sā mātrā sā kavalāḥ smṛtāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             asañcāryā tu yā mātrā <metamark function="yati">,</metamark>gaṇḍūṣa<cb/>ḥ sā
            prakīrttitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.63"> tāvac ca dhārayitavyo nanyamanasānunnatadehena yāvad
              doṣapratipūrṇṇagalaka<lb n="6"/>polatvan nāsāsrotronayanapariplavaś ca bhavati | tadā
            vimoktavyaḥ punaś cānyo grahītavyaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.64"> evaṃ snehapayaḥkṣaudrarasamūtrāmlasambhṛtāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kasāyoṣṇodakābhyāñ ca<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><pb n="323v"/><lb n="1"/> kavaḍā doṣato
            hitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.65"> vyādher apacayas tuṣṭi<metamark function="yati">,</metamark>r
            vviṣadaṃ vaktralāghavaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             indriyāṇām prasādaś ca <metamark function="yati">,</metamark> kavaḍe śuddhilakṣaṇaṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.66"> hīne jāḍyakaphotkleśā<metamark function="yati"
            >,</metamark>varasajñānam e<lb n="2"/>va ca |
            <caesura/>
             atiyogāt mukhe pākaḥ śoṣas tṛṣṇāruciklamāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.67">
            <cb/>śodhanīye viśeṣeṇa bhavaty etat tu lakṣaṇaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             tilān nīlotpalā<unclear reason="not sure if it is just a drop of ink">ṃ</unclear>
            sarppiḥ śarkkarā kṣīram eva <lb n="3"/>ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.68"> sakṣaudro dagdhavaktrasya gaṇḍūṣo dāhanāśana<metamark
              function="yati">,</metamark>ḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kava<cb/>lasya samāsena vidhir eṣa prakīrttitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.69"> vibhajya bheṣajam buddhyā kurvvīta pratisāraṇaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             ka<lb n="4"/>lko rasakriyā kṣaudraṃ cūrṇṇaṃ ceti caturvvidhaṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.70"> aṅgulyagrapraṇītan tu <metamark function="yati">,</metamark>
            yathāsvam mukharogiṇāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             tasya yogam ayogañ ca <metamark function="yati">,</metamark> kavaloktam vibhāvayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.71"> bhojaye<lb n="5"/>c cānabhiṣyandi <metamark function="yati"
              >,</metamark> doṣaghnam aśanan naram iti ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer"> || cikitsāsthāne catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>

            />tathā |
            <caesura/>
             netre pramāṇam vyāpac cā<metamark function="yati">,</metamark>nuvāsanasahottaraṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.73"> nirūhottarapīḍā ca <metamark function="yati">,,</metamark>
            dhūmanastena vai daśa || 0 || </l>
